      <h1 align="center">Tarver Woods Odds</h1> 
      <div class="author">
       Written by Jimmy Boyd
      </div> 
      <p>Antonio “Magic Man” Tarver takes on the Brit, Clinton Woods, on Saturday April 12th at St. Pete Times Forum in Tampa, Florida for the IBF/IBO Light Heavyweight Title. Jimmy Boyd weighs the Tarver-Woods odds in this fight night preview to help you with your boxing wagering. </p> 
      <p>Not surprisingly, Sportsbook.com lists Tarver as the -125 favorite, fighting in his home state of Florida, despite being the challenger. But how much magic will be left for the 39 year old fighter is the question we are considering here. Tarver is a former light heavyweight champion and is well known for being the first man to knock out Roy Jones Jr. Tarver is highly decorated with a professional record of 26-4 (19 wins by knockout).</p> 
      <p>Clinton Woods hails from Sheffield England. He finds himself as the underdog despite holding the IBF Light Heavyweight Title belt, which he earned in 2005 when he defeated Rico Hoye. Woods has an exceptional professional record of 41-3-1.</p> 
      <p>There’s no question that Tarver is the more popular fighter and the one the United States betting public will be pulling for. His rematch win over Roy Jones Jr. made him a celebrity. He made appearances on late-night shows and appeared on the cover of both Ring and KO Magazine. He was even a co-host on ESPN’s “Friday Night Fights.” In 2006, Tarver starred as Mason “The Line” Dixon, the heavyweight division champion in the last Rocky Film. I guess what I am getting at here is that Tarver is much more interested in the money that he can make now as opposed to the fighting. Tarver’s last serious fight came against Bernard Hopkins in June of 2006. Hopkins won as a 3-to-1 underdog, dominating the fight to win by unanimous decision. And I think you’ll see the dog barking again in this one as the younger Woods has the edge by my count.</p> 
      <p>As far as rounds go, I like this one to go the distance. Both fighters are very experienced and will not leave themselves open to a knockout.&nbsp;Take over 11.5 rounds at BodogLife.com.</p> 
      <p>Tarver  Woods Odds at Sportsbook.com</p> 
      <p>Tarver -125<br> Woods -105</p> 
      <p>Click on the <a href="http://www.locksmithsportspicks.com/boxing-odds/">boxing odds</a> link on the Locksmithsportspicks.com homepage to see which book has the best lines on this fight. Sign up for an account at any of Jimmy’s recommended houses to do you <a href="http://www.locksmithsportspicks.com">boxing betting</a> on the fight and receive the special signup bonuses that each particular book hands out. </p>

         <tr>
          <td colspan="3"><font size="+2"><strong>Loco Bandito</strong></font><br> Your basic lightweight racing shoe, no frills, no hype - just as flat and fast as a wheel measured downhill course. Guaranteed to take two minutes off your next 5K (gottcha - we're kidding of course). 
           <ul> 
            <li>Suggested List price: $100 (free shipping in New Zealand) </li> 
            <li>This model available until 2009 </li> 
           </ul> <p></p> <p>The Bandito is a no frills racing shoe built for the 5K and up with great forefoot cushioning and superb durability. </p> 
           <ul> 
            <li>Dual density EVA midsole </li>
            <li>Breathable mesh, speed laces for easy on/off </li>
            <li>Flexible - fully slip lasted </li>
            <li>Medial EVA post for just a dash of stability </li>
            <li>Solid carbon-rubber outsole for durability and traction </li>
           </ul> For LOCO runners who want an economical lightweight racing shoe with a distinctive look and responsive. <a href="#specs">More detailed specifications below photo! </a><br><br> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td colspan="3"><a href="images/bandito_1000.jpg"><img src="images/bandito_640.jpg" alt="" width="640" height="640" border="0"><br>Click on this photo for an even larger image.</a></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td colspan="3"><a name="specs"></a><font size="+2"><strong>LOCO BANDITO: Lightweight Racer, 231 grams, 8.2 oz.</strong></font> <p>The Bandito is a lightweight racing flat built to deliver a precise supportive fit and responsive cushioning while being as light and breathable as racing flats come. The Bandito will perform for distances from 5k to the marathon.</p> 
           <ul> 
            <li><strong>Anatomical last:</strong> The Bandito is constructed on a sleeker, more sculpted anatomical last. The sleek design of the last will fit the foot precisely from heel to forefoot for faster performance running. </li>
            <li><strong>Slip lasted:</strong> The Bandito is a fully slip lasted construction for maximum cushioning, lightweight, flexibility while offering a glove like fit throughout the shoe. </li>
            <li><strong>Upper design:</strong> The upper pattern is designed to be a minimal, low profile sleek design that's built for speed and comfort. With minimal overlays and more mesh the Bandito will be ultra light. The collar top line is soft and padded for comfort. </li>
            <li><strong>Upper materials:</strong> Air Mesh, High Density Synthetic, 3M webbing loops. 
             <ul> 
              <li> The vamp, tongue base and ankle collar is constructed with a state of the art air mesh. Air mesh is a tri layer material woven in one process that eliminates the need for cementing the layers together thus significantly improving breathability and comfort while reducing weight. </li>
              <li> The synthetic leather trim is an ultra thin (0.9mm), lightweight, soft and breathable synthetic that's extremely durable and flexible. The High Density NW backer is a high quality construction substrate. </li>
              <li> The 3M webbing loops are wide to aid in distributing even lace pressure distribution for a secure fit. The 3M strip on the lace loops and at the heel offer extra security for night time workouts. </li>
             </ul> </li>
            <li><strong>Laces:</strong> Yes flat laces. Back to functionality. Flat laces are easier to tie and stay tied. Round and oval laces become loose. </li>
            <li><strong>Midsole:</strong> The midsole of the Bandito is a lower profile anatomical tri density EVA. The heel is a higher durometer EVA for a more responsive feel so less energy and time is absorbed into the midsole. The forefoot is a softer EVA for cushioning with flex grooves while the medial post is positioned under the ankle for support. </li>
            <li><strong>Outsole:</strong> The outsole is a softer durometer compression molded carbon rubber. The softer durometer will enhance traction, especially on wet surfaces. The outsole design is a low profile unilateral mini lug pattern designed for traction and speed. The forefoot has cut out flex grooves to enhance flexibility. </li>
           </ul> <a name="footnote"></a><p>EVA is a copolymer or cross-linked foam made of ethylene and vinyl acetate. It is made up of hundreds of thousands of foam cells that contain air or gas. When you land on EVA foam you compress this EVA and the gas gets pushed out and then sucked back in again. Over time these cells don't rebound so well and don't take as much air back in. To compensate for this issue, a great majority of good running shoes use a compression molded EVA midsole. By compressing EVA in a pressurized mold the midsole forms a thick skin which helps the EVA last longer. It also provides structural rigidity to the midsole. </p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> </td> 
     </tr>

     <h1><strong>GRAND LODGE OF SCOTLAND</strong></h1> 
     <p>&nbsp;</p> 
     <div class="descr"> 
      <p>NATIONAL STRUCTURE</p> 
      <p>Scotland has the oldest lodges in the world. These are governed in Scotland by The <a href="http://www.grandlodgescotland.com" target="_blank">Grand Lodge of Scotland</a> or 'Grand Lodge' who meet in Freemason's Hall in Edinburgh. </p> 
      <p align="center"><img src="images/grand_lodge_arms.jpg" alt="Grand Lodge coat of arms" width="200" height="258"></p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p>

             <td valign="top" align="left" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" class="links"> 
              <div id="Titlelinks">
               <h1 class="pageTitle">Legal Services </h1>
              </div> 
              <div align="justify" class="h4">
                At<strong> Lodmell &amp; Lodmell,</strong> each <strong>Integrated Asset Protection Strategy</strong> is <strong>updated annually</strong> to ensure it keeps pace with your changing family, business, and financial circumstances. 
               <br> 
               <br> Developed by <strong>L&amp;L,</strong> one of the nation's premiere providers of asset protection services, the structures in each <strong>Integrated Asset Protection Strategy</strong> are customized to each client's needs. Included are layers of legal structures designed to <strong>preserve</strong> and <strong>protect</strong> your wealth from those predators who would take it away. 
               <br> 
               <br> <strong>L&amp;L's</strong> fee-based services begin with <strong>no obligation</strong> and a <strong>confidential review</strong> of your financial resources, and types of assets objectives. This analysis is followed by carefully crafted recommendations aimed at: 
               <br> 
               <br> 
               <ul> 
                <li>Establishing a <strong>legal barrier</strong> between the client and the client's assets; </li> 
                <li><strong>Insulating family wealth</strong> from potential liability by minimizing the economic incentive to sue; </li> 
                <li><strong>Deterring workplace lawsuits</strong> by requiring mandatory arbitration of disputes as a condition of employment; </li> 
                <li>Integrating new or existing asset protection into a solid legal strategy for protecting your net worth against attack, while <strong>avoiding unnecessary estate taxes</strong> and related costs. </li> 
               </ul> 
              </div> <span class="h4">If you have any clarification contact <a href="mailto:info@lodmell.com">info@lodmell.com</a></span> </td>

  <title>Blackhawk Stout</title> 
  <meta name="description" content="A tribute to Blackhawk Stout, a beer made in Sonoma County, California">

     <tr> 
      <td rowspan="3" width="150" height="400" bgcolor="white" align="left" valign="TOP"> <p> </p><h4><font face="helvetica" color="gray">Creative<br> Drifting<br> News<br> Sketchbook <p></p> </font><font face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="6"><b> </b></font></h4> </td>  
      <td width="425" height="400" align="LEFT" valign="TOP"> <p> <br> </p><h3>An Ode to Black Hawk Stout</h3> <p align="right"><font face="Courier New, Courier, mono" size="2">"Beer is proof that God loves us <br> and wants us to be happy."</font><font face="Courier New, Courier, mono"><br> <tt><br> —</tt> B<font size="2">ENJAMIN</font> F<font size="2">RANKLIN</font></font></p> <p><br> <img src="blackhawkstout-1.gif" width="235" height="300" hspace="10" vspace="2" align="left"> <tt><font face="Courier New, Courier, mono">I discovered something important today — or at least useful.</font> <font face="Courier New, Courier, mono">I was sketching near the pool and accidentally spilled Black Hawk Stout on my page. Before that, I had been soaking BFK Rives paper in coffee to get a tan color I like for relief prints. The stout achieved the same thing and is quicker. It was one of those happy accidents you hope for. So a proper tribute was required: <br> <br> Ah, Black Hawk Stout / You are good with food / You are good with trout / Oh, Black Hawk Stout / Some even say you are good for health / Could it be / You cure the gout / Ah, Black Hawk Stout / Oh, Black Hawk Stout / Have too much and you knock me out.<br> <br> The only problem is that 1 pint, 9.4 ounces of Black Hawk sells for about $3.65. I'll have to find out how many bottles it would take to fill a tub to dip a dozen sheets or so. I wonder if you can still drink the stuff afterward?<br> <br> P.S. Unfortunately, cheap mass produced lagers aren't dark enough or powerful enough to do the job.</font></tt><font face="Courier New, Courier, mono"><br> <br> </font><br> &lt; <a href="sketching.html">Back</a> | <a href="constructingapainting.html">Next </a> &gt; </p> 
       <hr> <br> <a href="sketchbook.html">Return to Sketchbook Table of Contents</a> <br> <p> <font size="2"><a href="index.html">Logan's Home Page</a> | <a href="profile.html">Profile</a> | <a href="mailto:logan@logansart.com">Guest Book (comments)</a> | <a href="links.html">Links</a></font><br> </p> </td> 
     </tr>

         <td width="100%" colspan="2"> <p class="paragraph_style" style="PADDING-TOP: 0pt" _extended="true"> <font face="Book Antiqua"> <span class="style_2" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 16px" _extended="true"><br> Our Alpaca farm is located just below the crest of the green rolling hills of East Albany Vermont in Vermont's "Northeast Kingdom". (between Newport and St. Johnsbury). The "Kingdom" is a very special place, far away from the hustle and bustle and a perfect place for raising very high quality Alpaca. Gently sloping hillsides covered with succulent green grasses from spring through fall, always fresh and clean mountain air and cool brisk winter temperatures where the snow still is measured in feet, all contribute to healthy and happy, densely fibered Alpaca champions. Explore our website to find out more about the charming and peaceful lifestyle that raising Alpacas allows. Call ahead if you would like to schedule a farm visit, if you are interested in purchasing one of our animals, or if you just want to talk 'paca. Log Cabin Farm Alpacas LLC is owned and operated by Jane &amp; John Nielsen<br> (<u>Please visit our site by clicking the blue link buttons on the left of the page)</u></span></font></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr>

    <div id="content"> 
     <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"> 
      <tbody> 
       <tr> 
        <td height="450" width="10%">&nbsp;</td> 
        <td valign="top" width="78%"> <p class="titles">Introduction</p> <p class="copy">LogiCity is a fun interactive computer game with a difference.&nbsp; Aimed at young people under 25, it's a game set in a 3D virtual city with five main activities where players are set the task of reducing the carbon footprint of an average resident.&nbsp; As players work their way through the game they will pick up information about Climate Change, and some of the main ways in which everyone is currently contributing to the emissions of the main greenhouse gas (CO2) that causes Climate Change.</p> <p class="copy">It places individuals in a virtual environment and lets them experiment and experience the potential effect that individual actions can have on the planet before it's too late. Users can travel to the future to see the direct results of their actions in real time by quickly fast forwarding to the year 2066. <br> <br> The game is part of Defra’s Climate Challenge programme to increase public awareness of Climate Change across the country.&nbsp; The National Energy Foundation, Logicom and British Gas are also providing some support to the game's development.<br> </p> <a href="http://www.logicity.co.uk/game" class="style3">Play the Game &gt;&gt;</a></td> 
        <td width="12%">&nbsp;</td> 
       </tr> 
      </tbody> 
     </table> 
    </div> 
    <div id="botnav">
     <img src="images/boticons.gif" usemap="#Map2" border="0" height="52" width="922"> 
    </div>

               <td valign="top" align="left" colspan="2">
                <div class="pghead1">
                 bulkSMS - Supported GSM Modems &amp; Phones
                </div></td> 
               <td valign="top" align="left"></td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td valign="top" colspan="4">&nbsp;</td> 
              </tr> 
              <tr> 
               <td valign="top" colspan="2">
                <div class="textC" style="width: 423; height: 209">
                  bulkSMS2.0 has been designed to work with any ETSI 07.05 compliant GSM Modem that supports sending and receiving of SMS in PDU mode.
                 <br> 
                 <br> Following is the list of GSM Modems &amp; Phone handsets with which bulkSMSwas tested successfully<font color="#FF0000">*</font>:
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a target="_blank" class="more" href="http://www.enfora.com"> Enfora</a>:</b>
                 <br> SA-EL, SA-G, SA-GL
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a target="_blank" class="more" href="http://www.falcom.de">Falcom</a>:</b>
                 <br> Twist, Swift, Samba 55, Samba 75
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a target="_blank" class="more" href="http://www.itegno.com">iTegno</a>:</b>
                 <br> WM1080A, WM1080A1I, WM1080A1E, 3000, 3232E, 3232I, 3898
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a target="_blank" class="more" href="http://www.multitech.com">Multitech</a>:</b>
                 <br> MTCBA-G-F1, MTCBA-G-F2, MTCBA-G-F4, MTCBA-G-UF1, MTCBA-G-UF2, MTCBA-G-UF4
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.nokia.com">Nokia</a>:</b>
                 <br> N12, N30, N32, 6100, 6210, 6220, 6310, 6310i, 6610, 6820(Bluetooth), 8250, 8910
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.siemens.com/index.jsp?sdc_p=pWMENcfst6u1436z1">Siemens</a>:</b>
                 <br> A65, AC75, AC45, C35, C45, ES75, M35, M45, MC35, MC35i, MC45, MC55, MC65, MC75,&nbsp; S35, TC35, TC35i, TC45, TC65
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.sim.com">SIMCOM</a>:</b>
                 <br> SIM100S, SIM100T
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.sonyericsson.com">Sony Ericsson</a>:</b>
                 <br> T226, T230, T238, T290, T310, T610, T630, T637, T68, T68i, K310, K320, K500, K510, K600, K700, K750i, K800i, W810, W900, S700, S710, V800, W300, W550, W600, W700, W800i, W810, W900, Z500, Z600, Z1010, GC75, GC79, GC83, GC85, GC89
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.teltonika.lt/en">Teltonika</a>:</b>
                 <br> T-ModemUSB, T-ModemCOM
                 <br> 
                 <br> <b> <a class="more" target="_blank" href="http://www.wavecom.com">Wavecom</a>:</b>
                 <br> Fastrack M1206B, Fastrack M1306B, Integra, WMOi3
                 <br> 
                 <br> 
                 <br> <font color="#FF0000">*</font> We strongly recommend that before purchasing the licensed version of bulkSMS you should check its compatibility with the modem you have or you intend to use it with. No refunds will be made for non-working of any GSM Modem (even if listed above) with bulkSMS

                    <td width="92%" valign="top"><p><img src="/images/stories/logoCreator_images/MacWin_smaller.png" border="0" align="right"></p><h1 align="right"> </h1><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p><h1 align="right">$29.95<a href="http://store.digitalriver.com/store/laughing/en_US/pd/ThemeID.2094900/productID.106748100"><img src="/images/stories/logoCreator_images/buy_sm.gif" border="0" align="right"></a></h1> </td> 
                   </tr> 
                   <tr> 
                    <td valign="top">
                     <div align="right">
                      <h2><span style="font-family: Times New Roman,Times,serif; font-size: 16px"><img src="/images/stories/logoCreator_images/qopen.gif" border="0"><em>.<span class="caption">..very cool effects that would require some serious design skills to create outside of The Logo Creator, and they look incredibly good!<img src="/images/stories/logoCreator_images/qclose.gif" border="0" width="36" height="26"></span></em></span></h2><span style="font-family: Times New Roman,Times,serif; font-size: 16px"> </span>
                     </div></td>

                 </div> <p><strong>The logos above are all generated from the same logo template! It's so easy to modify one logo to create many! </strong></p> <p>For any of you readers that are going to be venturing down the path of starting your own business, the process of coming up with a company name and designing a logo is one of the first steps of getting started. </p> <p>Traditionally I have always done <a href="http://www.thelogocreator.com/">logo design</a> for my companies using Photoshop, however Photoshop is major overkill if all youre looking for is an easy to use software package that just does logos. The Logo Creator 5.0 comes in a few different flavors. There is The Corporate Logo Edition, The Business Mascot Logo Edition, The Travel and Leisure Logo Design Set, The Entertainment Logo Edition, The Spiritual Logo Collection, The Real Estate Logo Edition, The Sports Logo Collection and The Mega Pak Logo Collection which basically includes all of the above.</p> <p>Essentially what you get with these software packages is an easy to use logo creation software package that comes pre-packaged with sample logo ideas for different market segments. You can see a sample of the kinds of logos that each package comes with so that you can decide which one best suits your needs.</p> <p>Here are a few samples from the different packages:</p> <p><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/spiritual/Logo_43_i.jpg" border="0" width="100" height="75"><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/Travel&amp;Leisure/Logo_03_i.jpg" border="0" width="100" height="75"><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/RealEstate/RE_Logo_18_i.jpg" border="0" width="100" height="75"><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/corporate/Logo_11_i.jpg" border="0" alt="4" width="100" height="75"><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/sports/Logo_37_i.jpg" border="0" alt="pythiaLogo" width="100" height="75"><img src="http://www.thelogocreator.com/Library_Sample_Logos/spiritual/Logo_45_i.jpg" border="0" alt="megapak5" width="100" height="75"></p> <p>So what you can basically do with the software is open up any one of these designs and just change the text within to reflect your company name. For example if you look at the first logo above which says Spiritual.com, I could easily replace that with InspiredMoneyMaker.com for example. It doesnt take long at all to do this and its pretty easy to get the hang of the software.<br> <br> I played around with it for about an hour and a half and I was able to whip up logo ideas really quickly based on the templates included. You dont have to use the pre-created templates, you could definitely create logos from scratch. </p> <p>At the end of the day, I personally dont feel comfortable using a pre-defined logo template for my needs as I dont want anyone else out there to have a similar logo to mine, so I would probably go through the process of using the software to design a logo from scratch, but you may be totally ok with utilizing some of the ideas included with the software for your needs. Keep in mind that the templates are just basic ideas. You can create anything you want with this, so you arent just limited to having a logo that looks like one of the ones that is included in the package.<br> <br> The website offers a free <a href="http://www.thelogocreator.com/demo.php" target="_blank">Downloadable Demo </a>version of the software that lets you try it for 30 days, as well as a <a href="http://www.thelogocreator.com/tutorials.html" target="_blank">tutorial section </a>which shows you how to use the software.</p> <p>I think if youre in the market for a logo design, and you dont want to pay a designer to do it for you, you might as well try this thing out to see if it does what you need unless youve already shelled out the money for a copy of Photoshop and you already know how to design your own logos in there.</p> <p>I dont know if Ill end up creating my logo in this software as I already own Photoshop, but if I didnt I would definitely take the time to go through the tutorials to see if this software would fit my needs.</p> </td>

 <body bgcolor="black" text="#FF6600" link="#FF6600" vlink="#FF6600" alink="#FF6600"> 
  <p style="margin-right:150; margin-left:0;" align="left"><img src="lohas.it/images/naturalstep1_html_smartbutton1.gif" namo_npi=":EmbededNPI1" border="0">&nbsp;</p> 
  <div id="layer1" style="width:486px; height:72px; position:absolute; left:211px; top:11px; z-index:1;"> <font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#CCCCCC"><!--NAMO_NAVBAR_START I h L       -1 6 7 5 4 3 --></font> 
   <div align="left"> <font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#CCCCCC"><a href="../index.htm" onmouseover="" onmouseout="">lohas.it</a>&gt;<a href="home.htm" onmouseover="" onmouseout="">home</a>&gt;<a href="environment.html" onmouseover="" onmouseout="">environment</a>&gt;<a href="keyconcepts.html" onmouseover="" onmouseout="">key concepts</a>&gt;<a href="naturalstep.html" onmouseover="" onmouseout="">natural step</a>&gt;natural1</font>
   </div> <font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#CCCCCC"><!--NAMO_NAVBAR_END--></font> 
  </div> 
  <p style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;" align="right"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#FF6600" size="5">The Four System Conditions</font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="5" color="#FF6600"> </font></p> 
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"> <b><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3">Through his work with child leukemia patients, Dr. Robert began to look at the sources of cancer that he found in the environment. However, Dr. Robert noticed that discussions of the links between the environment and health continually bogged down. This led him to engage in an extensive consensus process with 50 other scientists to find a set of irrefutable scientific principles on which to base his work. It is from those principles that Dr. Robert developed what are known as the Four System Conditions for sustainability.</font></b></p> 
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3"><b>In short, TNS addresses what we take, what we make, what we maintain, and how and what we share.</b></font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="3"> </font></p>
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3"><b>System condition one addresses what we take from the Earth's crust. It says that if we take metals, minerals and fossil fuels from the Earth faster than they can be recycled back into nature, these substances will build-up in the environment in problematic ways. We experience those problems in the form of smog, ozone depletion, global warming and poisoning from heavy metals like lead and mercury. Burning oil and coal faster than the trees can absorb the carbon is an example of violating the first system condition.</b></font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="3"> </font></p>
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3"><b>System condition two looks at the things we make and how well and quickly they can be reintegrated into the natural environment. Too much of anything, like garbage in land fills or sewage compromises the health of the natural system. There are also problems when we create synthetic chemicals nature can't break down quickly, like Styrofoam and plastics. Creating nuclear waste is an example of violating system condition number two.</b></font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="3"> </font></p>
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3"><b>System condition three is about maintaining the natural systems that support life. Everything comes from and goes back to the natural environment. All life, including humans, depend on these natural services: clean water and air, building materials and food. So system condition three says we need to restore and maintain these natural life support systems for our long term well-being.</b></font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="3"> </font></p>
  <p align="justify" style="margin-right:150; margin-left:50;"><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" color="#666666" size="3"><b>System condition four is about fairness and meeting the needs of all people and all species by using the most resource-efficient methods possible. If we don't meet the basic needs of everyone, through fair and efficient use of resources, it will be difficult or impossible to meet the other three conditions. Bananas and coffee grown on tropical plantations for sale in rich countries reflects problems with local food systems, loss of habitat and exploitation of cheap labor and so is an example of violating number four.</b></font><font face="Bradley Hand ITC" size="3"> </font></p>
  <p align="center" style="line-height: 100%; word-spacing: 0; margin-top: 3; margin-bottom: 2">&nbsp;<img src="lohas.it/images/naturalstep1_html_smartbutton2.gif" namo_npi=":EmbededNPI2" width="195" height="18" border="0"></p>  <!--Namo WebEditor Data 4.0

  <script>
// NS4-6,IE4-6
// Fade effect only in IE; degrades gracefully

// Set slideShowSpeed (milliseconds)
var slideShowSpeed = 3800

// Duration of crossfade (seconds)
var crossFadeDuration = 3

// Specify the image files
var Pic = new Array() // don't touch this
// to add more images, just continue
// the pattern, adding to the array below

Pic[0] = 'BG.gif'
Pic[1] = 'BG2.gif'
Pic[2] = 'BG3.gif'

var t
var j = 0
var p = Pic.length

var preLoad = new Array()
for (i = 0; i < p; i++){
   preLoad[i] = new Image()
   preLoad[i].src = Pic[i]
}

function runSlideShow(){
   if (document.all){
      document.images.SlideShow.style.filter="blendTrans(duration=2)"
      document.images.SlideShow.style.filter="blendTrans(duration=crossFadeDuration)"
      document.images.SlideShow.filters.blendTrans.Apply()      
   }
   document.images.SlideShow.src = preLoad[j].src
   if (document.all){
      document.images.SlideShow.filters.blendTrans.Play()
   }
   j = j + 1
   if (j > (p-1)) j=0
   t = setTimeout('runSlideShow()', slideShowSpeed)
}
</script>

// Get today's current date.
var now = new Date();

// Array list of days.
var days = new Array('Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday');

// Array list of months.
var months = new Array('January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December');

// Calculate the number of the current day in the week.

	return (number < 1000) ? number + 1900 : number;

              months[now.getMonth()] + " " +
               date + ", " +
                (fourdigits(now.getYear())) ;

          <td valign="top" height="413" bgcolor="#F7F3E7" colspan="2"> <p style="line-height: 100%; margin-left: 22; margin-right: 22"><font face="Arial" size="2"> <img border="0" src="LTCenter.jpg" align="right" hspace="7" width="282" height="194">The Lolo Trail Center is located 35 miles southwest of Missoula, Montana, on U.S. Hwy 12, along the Nez Perce Trail. It is completely surrounded by the wonderful nature that has always been the trademark of the beautiful Lolo National Forest. Alternately called the <i> Lolo Trail</i>, the <i> Nez Perce Trail</i> and the <i> Lewis and Clark Trail</i>, the 120-mile route from Lolo, Mont., to Weippe, Idaho, is a priceless historic artifact.<br> <br> In remembrance of the Expedition, as well as many other important historic elements of foregone days, we have constructed the Lewis and Clark Exhibition Center on our new 6000 square-feet addition to the property. Inside the Lewis and Clark Exhibition Center you'll experience a tribute to our magnificent history through a vast selection of art and crafts, as well as our wonderful library.<br> <br> <img border="0" src="LTCgrotto.jpg" align="left" hspace="6" width="214" height="173"> In addition, the Lolo Trail Center also has the grotto - featuring rock, log and slate construction with 13' and 18' flow-thru thermal pools of ceramic, not mud. Upstairs we have a conference center and library, Dinner Theatre, Wolf Den and gallery. Our gift shops are also one of a kind. The "Silver Nugget" has unique silver jewelry as well as antiques and other quality items that will make for a special memento of your stay with us. "The Lewis and Clark Exhibition Center" also displays a large variety of elegant historic and traditional souvenirs.</font></p><p style="line-height: 100%; margin-left: 22; margin-right: 22"><font face="Arial" size="2">Lolo Trail Center is a place where you can view replicas of Lewis &amp; Clark memorabilia (including their 1803 rifle), Mandan War axes, and many gift items from president Jefferson to the Indian Chiefs; a library-book store; many souvenir gift items; a mini-museum; displays by the Nez Perce, Salish and Kootenai Peoples and the U.S. Forest Service; and, collectibles including fine sculptures and art work.&nbsp;</font></p><p style="line-height: 100%; margin-left: 22; margin-right: 22"><font size="2" face="Arial">Here's an example of a piece of history that you can view, and purchase, at the Lolo Trail Center:</font></p><p style="line-height: 100%; margin-left: 22; margin-right: 22"><font face="Arial" size="2"> <img border="0" src="tomahawk.gif" align="right" hspace="8" vspace="8" width="230" height="164">A pipe tomahawk is a smoking pipe and tomahawk in one nifty tool!&nbsp; While the pipe tomahawk could be used as a weapon, if necessary, it was usually carried as a status symbol by influential members of a Native American tribe and used for smoking in different ceremonies. Merriwether Lewis had a pipe tomahawk which was lost at Canoe camp on the Clearwater River on October 7th 1805. The Corp of Discovery also carried twelve pipe tomahawks to be given as gifts. We too, carry accurately reproduced pipe tomahawks to be given as gifts. Come and see a piece of the Lewis and Clark journey at the Lolo Trail Center!<br><br></font> </p></td>

var clickmessage="Thank You For Visiting Lolo Trail Center!"

function disableclick(e) {
if (document.all) {
if (event.button==2||event.button==3) {
if (event.srcElement.tagName=="IMG"){
alert(clickmessage);
return false;
}
}
}
else if (document.layers) {
if (e.which == 3) {
alert(clickmessage);
return false;
}
}
else if (document.getElementById){
if (e.which==3&&e.target.tagName=="IMG"){
alert(clickmessage)
return false
}
}
}

function associateimages(){
for(i=0;i<document.images.length;i++)
document.images[i].onmousedown=disableclick;
}

if (document.all||document.getElementById)
document.onmousedown=disableclick
else if (document.layers)
associateimages()

        <tr> 
         <td valign="top"><img src="../img/vinpoz.gif" width="112" height="150" alt="" border="1" align="right"> <p align="justify">Giuseppe Silvestri, an important local writer,historian, journalist, introducing wine as a topic in his "La Valpolicella" a sort of Bible on the economic, cultural and social history of this valley, wrote in 1950: " The Valpolicella zone is greatly famous not so much for its breathtaking panoramas, its historic heritage or poets' lyrics, but for its wines ".<br> As a matter of fact these red celebrated wines played a leading role in the millenary history of the Valpolicella.<br> In Roman times RECIOTO was known as RETICUM, while in the origins ACINATICO was the name for AMARONE. Whatewer the origin, wines from Valpolicella are chief protagonists at table and are very generous, like the land where high quality grapes are grown.<br> It is a hilly lush area with tidy patches of vineyards, cherry orchards and olive groves, favoured by a mild tempered climate, with a soil rich in minerals.<br> The hillsides are protected to the north by the Lessini Mountains and the valley where Marano lies is a veritable paradise, a natural amphitheatre exposed to the sun from rising to sunset, opened towards the Veronese plain to the south.<br> Such is the zone where some delicate, deeply coloured, spicy wines are produced, each with a distinct character.<br> </p><br></td>
        </tr>

<html>
 <!-- InstanceBegin template="/Templates/page_template.dwt" codeOutsideHTMLIsLocked="false" --> 
 <head> <!-- InstanceBeginEditable name="doctitle" --> 
  <title>The LearningOnline Network with CAPA</title> <!-- InstanceEndEditable --> 
 </head> 
 <body bgcolor="#FFFFFF" link="#003333" alink="#339966" vlink="#229944" onload=""> 
  <table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="4" width="100%"> 
   <tbody>
    <tr bgcolor="#FFFF99"> 
     <td colspan="2" valign="top"><font color="#666666" size="6" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">The Learning<em>Online</em> Network with CAPA</font></td> 
    </tr> 
    <tr bgcolor="#CCCCCC"> 
     <td colspan="2"> <p><a href="index.html"><font face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Home</font></a><font face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"> <!-- InstanceBeginEditable name="URLList" -->&gt; <a href="download.html">Downloading and Installing</a> &gt; Before You Start<!-- InstanceEndEditable --></font><font color="#006600" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"> </font></p> </td> 
    </tr> 
    <tr> 
     <td colspan="2" bgcolor="#FFFFFF"><h1><font color="#006600" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><!-- InstanceBeginEditable name="title" -->Before You Start<!-- InstanceEndEditable --></font></h1> <font face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><!-- InstanceBeginEditable name="MainBody" --> <p><img src="dcpics/mark_wolfgang_ed_guy.jpg" width="300" height="227" align="right">LON-CAPA is a complex software system. Before you start installing it on a machine, please be aware of the following issues.</p> <h3>LON-CAPA is free?</h3> <p>LON-CAPA is free, <a href="http://www.gnu.org/philosophy/free-sw.html"><em>both</em> as in "free speech" <em>and</em> in "free beer."</a> Neither for the software nor the cluster membership do you have to pay us or any other third party. But running LON-CAPA is not for free - you will need to buy a server (the least of all costs), and dedicate time, energy, and human resources to the maintainance of the system and the support of your faculty and students. In terms of server maintainance, we expect our cluster members to keep the operating system updated and secure, and install new versions of LON-CAPA as they become available. We do offer on-site installation and remote maintainance support for a fee, as well as hosting services.</p> <h3>Dedicated server</h3> <p>Like most other CMS and LCMS systems, LON-CAPA should be run on a dedicated machine for easier maintenance, higher security, better performance, and to avoid interference and conflicts with other applications. All <a href="http://install.lon-capa.org/">installation scripts</a> expect a dedicated machine with only a minimal operating system installation.</p> <h3>Operating system</h3> <p>The LON-CAPA installation is optimized for <a href="http://fedora.redhat.com/">Fedora</a>, <a href="http://www.novell.com/linux/">SUSE</a>, and <a href="http://www.redhat.com/rhel/">Redhat Enterprise</a>, and we strongly encourage system administrators to use a recent version of one of these three distributions. We are running local installations of these distributions in production, so we are more ready to assist you should you encounter problems. People have gotten LON-CAPA to work on Debian and other Linux distributions, but you will be in for surprises and glitches, and we will not be able to help you much. </p> <h3>Will the LON-CAPA server software work on the Solaris box I found?</h3> <p>No.</p> <h3>Will the LON-CAPA server software work under MacOS X Server? FreeBSD?</h3> <p>Currently not, but we would really love to make this work. There is no reason why LON-CAPA should not run on MacOS X or FreeBSD, but installation <strong>will be painful</strong>. This is due to the large number of libraries we are using, as well as the fact that some packages will need re-compilation, and that the organization of the file system is different. <strong>YOU HAVE BEEN WARNED!</strong> As you might decide to work on this, please work with us. And if you get this to work, your detailed notes and binaries would be very much appreciated.</p> <h3>Will the LON-CAPA server software work under Windows?</h3> <p>No, and we are not planning on it, either. Since we are making use of many operating system specific libraries and features, the required effort to port the LON-CAPA software to Windows will be tremendous.</p> <h3>Now I am confused. I cannot use Windows?</h3> <p>It's important to distinguish between the LON-CAPA server software, and the client. You can use LON-CAPA with most any browser on most any platform. But the server software needs to run on a Linux server.</p> <h3>I have this discarded office PC sitting around ...</h3> <p>Who doesn't? Fact is, the LON-CAPA server software will work on almost any old PC that runs Linux, but not in production mode. Please check out our <a href="hardware.html">hardware recommendations</a>. Servers that actually hold student performance data (i.e., library servers) must have backup, either over the network or on tape.</p> <h3>Static IP Address</h3> <p>LON-CAPA servers must have a static IP address, and reverse-DNS-lookup must work for that address.</p> <h3>I want to frequently move the server around</h3> <p>Not a good idea. You should really get an IP address and hostname for your server, and stay with it. The reason is that you probably want to join a LON-CAPA cluster, and the hostname and IP is what your server is going to be registered under. In order for the other machines in the network to trust yours, you need to keep your address, and your DNS server must own up to it.</p> <h3>Firewalls</h3> <p>LON-CAPA needs several ports open, namely 80, 8080, and 5663. If you want us to assist you remotely, please also keep port 22 open for ssh. Also, IP masking causes severe problems and will require lots of custom configuration. </p> <h3>LON-CAPA says it cannot connect</h3> <p>Well ... see above.</p> <h3>There is nothing there ...</h3> <p>LON-CAPA is designed as a networked system from the ground up. If you install your machine "standalone," you really see hardly any advantages in what it does. To become useful, your machine needs to be connected to a cluster. We are maintaining two clusters, the development and the <a href="clustermap.html">production cluster</a>, which establishes the <a href="sharedpool.html">shared content repository</a>. <font color="#FF0000">If you plan on connecting your machine to the production cluster (install option "production"), you must contact <a href="mailto:lon-capa@lon-capa.org">lon-capa@lon-capa.org</a> for an assignment of LON-CAPA domain and machine name <strong>first</strong></font> - the MSU group acts as the gatekeeper for the <a href="consortium.html">LON-CAPA Academic Consortium</a>. We will need your server data, administrative contact, etc, verify your identity, and then modify the cluster tables. Changes will eventually be propagated across the network, and only then will you be able to see the other machines.</p> <h3>Do you accept anybody into the LON-CAPA cluster?</h3> <p>Nope. We have a responsibility to the authors of the resources in the system to preserve the integrity of the pool. The Board of the LON-CAPA Academic Consortium votes on acceptance into the pool. Generally, we do expect your institution to be a solidly established school, college, or university. Also, we will need a verifiable administrative contact, who is faculty or staff of your institution. Your emails from penguindude@yahoo.com will likely not receive an unquestioned welcome - nothing personal.</p> <h3>What are my responsibilities as a node on the LON-CAPA cluster?</h3> <p>You need to</p> <p> </p>
       <ul> 
        <li>keep the machine secure (i.e., update the OS and LON-CAPA regularly)</li> 
        <li>prevent unauthorized access to the machines</li> 
        <li>protect the LON-CAPA resource pool from public access and source-level exploits</li> 
        <li>have the server up and running at least 95% of the time</li> 
       </ul> <p>In other words, we want to see your server professionally maintained. It's not that hard.</p> <p></p> <h3>Can I get kicked out of the cluster?</h3> <p> </p><p>You bet, if you don't do the above! However, the Board will (except in emergencies, and we don't know at the moment what those would be) notify you first and ask you to correct the situation within a reasonable timeframe.</p> <h3>Is LON-CAPA backward compatible to CAPA or Lecture<em>Online</em>?</h3> <p>LON-CAPA has a question format that is different from both CAPA and Lecture<em>Online</em>, but there are <a href="capaupgrade.html">scripts to translate the questions</a>. All MSU material has already been translated, and so have all of the <a href="publisher.html">publisher textbook libraries</a> - as part of the network, you would have immediate access to these libraries. If there is material developed at your institution, which needs translation, we can assist, and run the scripts for you.</p> <h3>Where do I find documentation?</h3> <p>Documentation can be found on the <a href="http://install.lon-capa.org/">main installation site</a>, as well as in our <a href="http://help.lon-capa.org/fom/cache/4.html">FAQ-O-Matic</a>. You can also join or browse our <a href="http://mail.lon-capa.org/mailman/listinfo/lon-capa-admin">system administrator mailing list</a>.</p> <h3>But I cannot get it to work ...</h3> <p>The last thing we want you to do is sit around and complain about LON-CAPA, or even give up. Send us an email! We are pretty busy here, but within our capacity, please let us assist you. Please send email to <a href="mailto:lon-capa@lon-capa.org">lon-capa@lon-capa.org</a>.</p> <!-- InstanceEndEditable --> </font> <p>&nbsp;</p></td> 
    </tr> 
    <tr> 
     <td bgcolor="#FFFF99"><p><font color="#666666" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif">Contact Us: </font><font face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif"><a href="mailto:korte@lon-capa.org">lon-capa@lon-capa.org</a></font></p> </td> 
     <td width="102" bgcolor="#FFFF99"><p><img src="images/lonlogotrans.gif" width="100" height="67" align="right"></p></td> 
    </tr> 
   </tbody>
  </table>  <!-- InstanceEnd --> WARC/0.18 WARC-Ty
 </body>
</html>

      <h1>TECHNICAL ADVICE </h1> 
      <h2> <a name="focusinterview"></a>Services for Start-up and Micro-Food Companies </h2> 
      <p><br> The London Food Centre runs a ‘Focus Interview’ service at a subsidised rate. Especially designed for supporting start-up and micro-businesses, the session is a chance to meet the experts and ask advice on food technology, food labelling, shelf life, storage and numerous important issues.<br> Many individuals with an idea have used LFC’s focus interview to take the next step forward – many are now successful companies. Use our interviews to signpost your next step!<br> <br> <img src="images/focus_interview.gif" alt="Focus Interview" width="410" height="133"></p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <p><a href="consultancy.shtml">For staff expertise follow this link </a></p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      <br> 
      <p></p>

    <table height="1673" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="5" width="794" align="left" border="0">

      <tr align="middle"> 
       <td width="1" height="107" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolor="#FF6699" bordercolorlight="#FF6699" bordercolordark="#FF6699">&nbsp; </td> 
       <td width="466" height="107" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolor="#FF6699" bordercolorlight="#FF6699" bordercolordark="#FF6699"> <p align="justify" style="word-spacing: 0">&nbsp; </p><p align="justify" style="word-spacing: 0">&nbsp; </p><p align="justify" style="word-spacing: 0"> </p></td>
       <td width="290" height="107" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left"> <p align="right">&nbsp; </p><p align="right">&nbsp; </p><p align="right"> <font face="Xerox Sans Serif Wide" size="5" color="#FF6699">&nbsp;food in the arts </font> </p><p align="right"> <font color="#FF6699"> &nbsp;</font></p></td>

      <tr align="middle"> 
       <td width="1" height="30" bgcolor="#CC0066" align="left">&nbsp; </td> 
       <td width="760" colspan="2" height="30" bgcolor="#CC0066" align="left">&nbsp; </td> 
       <td width="0" height="30" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left">&nbsp; </td> 
      </tr> 
      <tr align="middle"> 
       <td width="1" height="32" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF">&nbsp; </td> 
       <td width="760" colspan="2" height="32" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF">&nbsp; </td> 
       <td width="0" height="32" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF">&nbsp; </td> 
      </tr> 
      <tr align="middle"> 
       <td width="1" height="1460" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF"> <p style="margin-left: 2px; margin-top: 0">&nbsp; </p></td> 
       <td width="760" colspan="2" height="1460" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF"> 
        <table width="766" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="10" height="1319" class="ms-simple1-main" style="border-top-style: solid; border-bottom-style: solid"> 
         <tbody>
          <tr valign="top"> 
           <td height="21" class="ms-simple1-left"> <p style="margin-left: 2px; margin-top: 0"> <font color="#800080" face="Lucida Sans Unicode" size="3">WARSAW/ <a href="../Artmai~1/Artist's%20Films.htm">ARTISTS 1650-1899</a>/ <a href="../Artmai~1/Mainar~1.htm">ART MAIN</a></font> </p></td> 
           <td width="168" height="21" align="right" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF" class="ms-simple1-even"> <b><a href="../Main.htm"><font color="#CC0066" size="2" face="Arial">home</font></a></b></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr valign="top"> 
           <td width="558" height="302" rowspan="3" class="ms-simple1-left"> <img border="0" src="../IMAGES/warsaw-2.jpg" width="464" height="379"></td> 
           <td width="168" height="39" align="right" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF" class="ms-simple1-even"> <p style="margin-left: 2px; margin-top: 0"> <b> <a href="../FILMMA~1/Mainfi~1.htm"> <font color="#CC0066" size="2" face="Arial">film and food</font></a><font size="2"> </font></b> </p></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr valign="top"> 
           <td width="168" height="39" align="right" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF" class="ms-simple1-even"> <p align="right"><b><font face="Arial" size="2" color="#CC0066"> <a href="../Literature%20Main/Main.htm"><span class="style1">literature and food</span></a></font><font size="2"><a href="../Literature%20Main/Main.htm"><span class="style1"> </span></a></font></b></p> </td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr valign="top"> 
           <td width="168" height="248" align="right" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF" class="ms-simple1-even"> <p style="margin-left: 2px; margin-top: 0"> <b> <a href="../Musicm~1/Mainmu~1.htm"> <font color="#CC0066" size="2" face="Arial">music and food</font></a><font size="2"> </font></b> </p></td> 
          </tr> 
          <tr valign="top"> 
           <td height="927" class="ms-simple1-left"> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">‘<b>Do you know what fills me most with wonder?’&nbsp; the Head of the Music School asked. ‘The powerlessness of the police to do anything about it.' They were conspicuously absent at his funeral. And four months later they still wouldn’t dare come within five hundred metres of the place.</b></font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <b> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></b></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">We had spent early Monday evening buying sheet music at a shop close to the Opera House where, the previous Friday, we had been given presidential treatment in the form of two front balcony seats to <i>La Fille Mal Garde</i>. Our host failed to secure the benefits of privilege a second time. We missed a concert of Mozart and drove north to the church or St. Stanislav Kostka. As we parked in the square, candlelit faces were passing upturned green benches behind the railings.</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left">&nbsp;</p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">This was the diocese of Father Jerzy Popieluszki. The church itself is modern, with twin frontal towers reminiscent of a design by Borromini and Rainaldi, surrounded by a little land, in one corner of which a kiosk sold photographs and mementos. Nearby, candles burned before a fortress of pine branches, an abundance of flowers lay on the mound of a recent grave, which seemed exceptionally high. They must have either dug deep or carried barrows of earth from elsewhere. On the funeral day, messages from international Solidarity had pointed outwards, but within a short time, notices of condolence began to replace threats of aggression. An illegal anchor built of twigs rested against the railings, no longer turned defiantly outwards but inwards towards the church. The open boot of a Polish Fiat, contained a Christ effigy, surrounded by three black shrouds hung from sticks.</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent3" style="tab-stops: 67.7pt 103.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent3" style="tab-stops: 67.7pt 103.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">Visiting clerics were melancholic and hopeful. A dismal silence and a mindless authority had been broken. Within this protected area grayness lifted from faces, at once startled by new words and phrases flowing into a long-interrupted conversation. The shrine of Popieluszki is not a symbol. The Poles will not win their democracy with symbols. </font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <b> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">To the left of the church young men wearing yellow armbands patrol the grounds. Inside a balconied apartment - the home of the former incumbent - the lights are turned on. Within the body of the church, the congregation overflows through the doors. Their eyes are burning with excitement. Electrified, they realise that, despite the safety in numbers, if they close the church now or if they extinguish the light, all might be lost. More candles burn, new arrivals walk down the aisles, kneel and cross themselves in silence. Not one cough is heard, or whispered prayer or lamentation. No comment, word of greeting, welcome or sign of recognition. A sense of fraternity creeps through&nbsp; this manifestation and steals its anonymity. More people file past the open doors while others return to the pitch black outside.</font></span></b></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">The following day, within sight of Lazienki, compacted snow lies over the Botanical Gardens. Motorised ploughs push along the arbours, dislocating floating eyes beneath their tread. Nuns from the convent walk by wearing fashionable boots. They are young and businesslike. Their looks thrive. Ahead of them the path comes out of the wood and meanders alongside a lake. The island has not thawed out and wild fowl huddles on its shelf. In the distance the roof of the Music School is visible. Students return from a lecture and pensioners walk their dogs. Where do they imagine is the ideal place to live? </font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> &nbsp;</p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="en-us"><font size="2">Before </font></span> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">a concert of chamber music at the Palace a woman speaks loudly and writes something in a diary. She is not a critic. The audience stares at this lonely figure, who hums the violin part as the musicians continue to play. During the interval I walk back to the old town. Fresh snow flurries in my face. I pull up my collar and push against the blizzard. At the entrance to St. John’s Cathedral two oil lamps burn behind a window. I blow into my gloved hands. Dziekania Street is laden with snow. An avalanche tips off the flying balcony that links the castle with the royal stall in the cathedral chancel. The gutters in Kanonia Square are frozen.</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">Above the Kamienne Schodki cafe plumes grey smoke. I venture down the stone steps and wander inside the bookshop, formerly a printers, where, in the eighteenth century, Warsaw’s first daily newspaper, Gazeta Rzadowa, was published . My breath does not disappear. The temperature is fourteen below zero and these little clouds just hang around my face. Inside the bookshop, my friends browse as quiet as mice. An inner voice laughs in delight. A candle flame leans back in surprise. </font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left">&nbsp; </p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2"><b>There is no such escape from exile. Unforeseeable laws govern the globe. It is futile to complain: there is no distance, there is no longer an inside or an outside. Is not the sail of every doctrine inflated with revolution? Are there not basic laws within each of us about which almost everybody would agree? An exile is a refugee from the community in which he no longer lives. An alien is severed from his connections and is repudiated by all. What are we all, but aliens and exiles too</b>? </font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">&nbsp;</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2">Popieluszki was hoping to contribute to the growth of society.</font></span></p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left">&nbsp; </p> <p class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="tab-stops: 59.8pt 88.7pt; text-autospace: none; font-family: Arial; margin-left: 2px; margin-right: 0cm; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: .0001pt" align="left"> <span lang="EN-US"><font size="2"><i>T</i><i>imothy Foster - unpublished -1985</i></font></span></p></td> 
           <td width="168" height="927" align="right" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF" class="ms-simple1-even">&nbsp;</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>
        </table>  </td> 
       <td width="0" height="1460" bgcolor="#FFFFFF" align="left" bordercolor="#FFFFFF" bordercolorlight="#FFFFFF" bordercolordark="#FFFFFF">&nbsp; </td> 
      </tr>    
     </tbody>
    </table> 
    <p>&nbsp;</p> 
   </center>
  </div>  WARC/0.18 WARC-T

        <tr>
         <td> <span class="Default">
           <table class="Default" width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td align="Left"><strong>Fronwydyr (The club hut)</strong></td>
              <td align="Right"></td>
             </tr>
            </tbody>
           </table> </span>
          <hr><span class="Default"> <p>The London Mountaineering Club owns a club hut, called 'Fronwydyr'.</p> <p>It is located in the Snowdonia national park near Llanberis, in North Wales. It sleeps 16 people, has three bedrooms, a living room, a kitchen, a drying room and showers. It is available to members and their guests via the club's Hut Booking Secretary at extremely reasonable rates.</p> <p></p><h2>Booking the Hut</h2><p></p> <p>The hut is available for hire by legitimate organizations (clubs, schools etc). The minimum size of such a group booking is 10 members, and proof of status is required.</p> <p>For all hut bookings, please <a href="asp/SendMail.asp?sendto=Hut+Booking+Secretary">click here to contact Helen, the Hut Booking Secretary</a> or by phone on 07968 338 997</p> <p><b></b></p><h2><b>Rates</b></h2><p></p> 
           <table class="Data" border="1" id="Table1"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td>Members</td>
              <td> per person per night</td>
             </tr> 
             <tr>
              <td>Guests</td>
              <td>.00 per person per night</td>
             </tr> 
             <tr>
              <td>Bookings by outside parties/clubs/organisations</td>
              <td>.00 per person per night</td>
             </tr> 
             <tr>
              <td>Day rate (for use of showers/kitchen)</td>
              <td>50p per person per day</td>
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> <p><b></b></p><h2><b>How to get there</b></h2><p></p> <p>You can also download directions to the hut in PDF format by <a href="/downloads/fronwydyr.pdf">clicking here</a></p> Fronwydyr (grid reference: 606587) is located in the village of Nant Peris.<br> 
           <ul> 
            <li>You can either take the M1 or M40 out of London to join the M6 northbound. If taking the M40, turn off at the M42 Junction 3A (northbound), to join the M6 northbound.</li> 
            <li>From the M6, after passing Birmingham, turn onto the M54 at junction 10A towards Telford.</li> 
            <li>The M54 will end and become the A5. From the start of the A5, follow this for 78 miles/125 km, passing Llangollen, Corwen and Betws-y-coed to get to Capel Curig.</li> 
            <li>At Capel Curig, turn left onto the A4086 (passing the Plas-y-Brenin outdoor centre).</li> 
            <li>4.5 miles/7 km from Capel Curig, you will see a small building on the right. This is the famous Pen-y-Gwryd hotel (See map below).</li> 
            <p><img src="images/snowdonia_map.jpg"><br> <small><i>Image produced from the Ordnance Survey <a href="http://www.ordnancesurvey.co.uk/getamap">Get-a-map</a> service. Image reproduced with kind permission of <a href="http://www.ordnancesurvey.co.uk/">Ordnance Survey</a> and <a href="http://www.osni.gov.uk/">Ordnance Survey of Northern Ireland</a>.</i></small></p> 
            <li>Turn right at the hotel and travel for 4.5 miles/7 km into Nant Peris (passing the Pen-y-Pass YHA on the way).</li> 
            <li>The only pub in Nant Peris is the Vaynol Arms (refer to map below). Opposite the pub is a campsite.</li> 
            <li>There is a right turn on to a narrow gravel road 100 metres after the pub (with a stone building on the corner).</li> 
            <li>Another 100 metres up the gravel road, you will get to a junction. Straight ahead takes you to the campsite or turn left towards Fronwydyr.</li> After turning left, travel uphill for 200 metres, passing a few buildings on the left. 
            <li>You will finally get to a gate on the left, marked "Fronwydyr"</li> 
           </ul> <p>Fronwydyr has parking space for about 6 cars.</p> <p><b>Please note that Fronwydyr has very poor mobile reception, so don't rely on being able to ring up for directions.</b></p> <img src="images/fronwydyr_map.jpg"> <p>You can also download directions to the hut in PDF format by <a href="/downloads/fronwydyr.pdf">clicking here</a></p> </span></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="Default" width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <td align="Right"></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> </td>
    </tr>

     <td colspan="2" align="Center"><small> &nbsp;&nbsp; LMC 1.4 05/11/05 </small></td>

   <div id="content"> 
    <div class="right">
     <span class="style9">"Simply World Class" is the description made by the Germany press of the London Piano Trio. For the past decade the London Piano Trio have been touring, recording, and teaching across the globe to rave reviews. At home they have been described as a " National Treasure". They are all committed teachers <font size="3"><font size="2">and current </font></font> activities include residencies at the Danbury Festival, UK, and the Certosa International Festival, Capri, Italy</span> 
     <div class="articles">
      <br> 
      <hr> <span class="style14"><font color="#333333">News of the trios forthcoming activities can be viewed in the concerts section.</font></span>

							_args[i] = _args[i].split("}");
							form.args += eval(_args[i][0]) + _args[i][1];
						}
					}
					form.args = form.args.replace(/ /g,"");
					_win = window.open('',form.target,form.args);
					if(typeof(focus)=="function")
					_win.focus();
					return true;
				}
						//-->
		</script>

             <o:p> 
             </o:p> </font></span></p> <p align="left"><font face="Arial" size="2"><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-font-family: Times New Roman; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; mso-fareast-language: EN-US;       <p align="right"> <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/the_real_of_the.html">« the real of the desert</a> | <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/">Main</a> | <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/long_sunday_dia.html">Long Sunday Dialogues »</a> </p> 
      <h3>"Critique of Violence" Roundup</h3> 
      <p>By <em>populist</em> demand: the Long Sunday Symposion on Walter Benjamin's "Critique of Violence".</p> 
      <p>The <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/symposium_on_cr.html">Call For Contributors</a> and the <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/schedule_for_cr.html">Schedule</a> and the <a href="http://archive.blogsome.com/2005/11/22/walter-benjamin-violence/">best plug</a>.</p> 
      <ul>
       <li>Jon BeasleyMurray <a href=" http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/critique_of_vio.html">"'Critique of Violence' and the Party Form"</a></li> 
       <li>Matt Christie <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/chora.html">"Chora"</a></li> 
       <li>Jodi Dean <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/divine_violence.html">"Divine Violence"</a></li> 
       <li>Adam Kotsko <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/_the_following_.html">"'Critique of Violence and Deconstruction"</a></li> 
       <li>Marc Lombardo <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/marc_lombardo_o.html">"Language, Jurisprudence and the Divine"</a></li> 
       <li>Craig McFarlane <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/the_three_names.html">"The Three Names of Power"</a></li> 
       <li>Angela Mitropoulos <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/benjamin_gewalt.html">"Benjamin, geWalt"</a></li> 
       <li>Paul Passavant <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/paul_passavant_.html">"Foucault as a Critique of Benjamin"</a></li> 
       <li>Kenneth Rufo <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/the_auratic_eco.html">"The Auratic Economy of a Critique of Violence"</a></li> 
       <li>Alain Wittman <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/11/pure_means.html">"Pure Means"</a></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Off-site discussion: <a href="http://archive.blogsome.com/2005/12/06/benjamin-afformative">Archive</a> (<a href="http://archive.blogsome.com/2005/12/01/walter-benjamin-longsunday">Another</a>); <a href="http://jdeanicite.typepad.com/i_cite/2005/12/not_all_is_subj.html">I Cite</a>; <a href="http://fortkant.blogspot.com/2005/12/party-form.html">Fort Kant</a>; <a href="http://www.adamkotsko.com/weblog/2005/12/universalizing-divine-law.html">The Weblog</a>; <a href="http://whatinthehell.blogsome.com/2005/12/11/88/">What in the hell...</a>; <a href="http://epideixis.blogspot.com/2005/12/long-sundays-critique-of-violence.html#links">Epideixis</a></p> 
      <p>(Should anyone have links to any other discussion of the symposium elsewhere, please leave a comment.)</p> <a id="more"></a> 
      <p class="posted"> By Craig | December 11, 2005 in <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/benjamin/">Benjamin</a>, <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/symposia/">Symposia</a> | <a href="http://www.long-sunday.net/long_sunday/2005/12/critique_of_vio_1.html">Permalink</a> </p>

function jumpPage(totalPage,path,params)
{
	var pageNo=document.all("pageNo").value;
	var pageRegExp=/^[\d]+$/;
	if(!pageRegExp.test(pageNo)||parseInt(pageNo)>totalPage||parseInt(pageNo)<1)
	{
		alert("Please input 1"+totalPage+"");
		document.all("pageNo").select();
		return false;
	}
	if(params.length>0)
		params="&"+params;
	window.location.href=path+"?pageNo="+pageNo+params;
}
</script>

                 <td width="562" height="230" valign="bottom" class="grayy"><span style="color: #ffcc00">Pasta</span> ( <a href="cpjj-bbyf1.asp">about Pasta click here.... </a>)<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pasta has more than 500 kinds, including Spaghetti, Farfalle, Capellini, Fusilli, Tagliatelle, and etc. Any gastronomy can make palatable cuisines. It is reported that, pasta, with carbohydrate, protein, and Vitamins, which reduces in the level of LDL (bad) cholesterol and improves coronary artery, is suitably served to athletes before competition. Furthermore, with higher nutrition and lower calories, pasta helps the metabolism and accumulate energy.<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pasta is the Italian dish by excellence. The Italian dish by excellence is, deservedly, the main-style of Mediterranean cuisine. The secret lies in combing its already good nutritional properties with its satiating capacity, without increasing the calories intake with excessively fat dressings. Pasta, actually, even though it is not a complete food by itself, needs very little to become one. To balance it, you just need to add a sauce that may be made of vegetables, proteins (without exaggerating) and fats. Furthermore, it shall have to be al dente and not only for taste reasons: to chew more means removing hunger and digesting better.<br> </td> 
                 <td width="215" align="center" valign="middle"><img src="../cn/images/cjjs1.jpg" width="200" height="200" class="style"></td> 
                </tr> 
               </tbody>
              </table></td> 
             <td width="6" rowspan="8" align="center" valign="middle"></td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td align="left" valign="middle" class="grayy">
              <table width="780" border="0"> 
               <tbody>
                <tr> 
                 <td valign="top" class="grayy">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;But what are the reasons behind this dish becoming almost the symbol of the Mediterranean diet? It is its capacity to release the starches very slowly, thus allowing to modulate their effect on the organism. In other words, the feeling of being full lasts longer, whereas the sensation of hunger, after a dish of pasta, returns much later than with other cereal-based dishes such as pizza, bread or rice. <br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Another advantage of the slow assimilation of pasta concerns the sugars that are contained, which, if metabolized too rapidly, would cause dangerous repercussions on glycemia. A factor to be kept in mind, and not only for diabetics. <br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Finally, a dish of spaghetti dressed with tomato, basil, extra virgin olive oil, and one sprinkle of Parmigiano Reggiano, is not only a typical product of Italian tradition, but a correct meal from a nutritional view point. <br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, Barilla, using 100% best-quality durum wheat as ingredient, become the top pasta maker in the world. </td> 
                </tr> 
               </tbody>
              </table></td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td height="6" align="left" valign="top"></td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td align="left" valign="middle"></td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td align="left" valign="middle">
              <table width="780" border="0"> 
               <tbody>
                <tr> 
                 <td width="215" rowspan="3" align="center" valign="middle"><img src="../cn/images/cjjs2.jpg" width="200" height="200" class="style"></td> 
                 <td width="552" class="grayy">Pasta allows every day to combine the pleasure of eating well with being well. Because pasta:<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* is complete and balanced. Rich in carbohydrates, when seasoned with typical ingredients of the Mediterranean cuisine, and thus paired with proteins, fats and vitamins, it is a nutritionally balanced food;<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* is easily digested. It does not make digestion heavy and it allows you to feel light and lively;<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* is full of energy. The energy of its carbohydrates is gradually released in order to give you the right charge in any moment of the day;<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* is ideal in the diet. It satisfies for long letting you control the caloric intake and limit excesses;<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* is great with every recipe. Thanks to its versatility, it satisfies the palate in a thousand different ways, giving you full pleasure with each forkful. </td> 
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td height="6" class="grayy"></td> 
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td class="grayy"><span style="color: #FFCC00">A grain of wheat and a great company</span><br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Attention to wheat has long been a basic priority for Barilla.</td> 
                </tr> 
               </tbody>
              </table></td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td>
              <table width="780" border="0"> 
               <tbody>
                <tr> 
                 <td class="grayy">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In 1961, this Parma-based company employed its first agronomist, thereby initiating what was to become an important line of activity Euro Research to improve the quality of plants and to extend the cultivation of durum wheat to northern Italy form the centre and south.<br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Barilla is today the world's largest consumer of wheat for the production of pasta and baked products. Just to give an idea of how much, consider that the surface required to cultivate all the wheat used by the company in a year is equal to 12,000 basketball courts!</td> 
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td height="5" class="grayy"></td> 
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td class="grayy"><span style="color: #ffcc00">Pasta Sauce</span> (<a href="cpjj-bbyf2.asp">about Pasta Sauce click here....</a> ) <br> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Barilla Pasta Sauce are for these who pursuit the real Mediterranean tradition flavor. Moreover, Barilla Pasta Sauces are prepared only with carefully selected ingredients, bringing on your table the fragrant aroma of basil, the gravy and deliciousness of Bolognese, the concentrated flavor of olive, or sweetness and hot of bell pepper. </td> 
                </tr> 
               </tbody>
              </table></td> 
            </tr>

             <td>
              <table width="780" border="0">
